Go here. Chris and his brother (I didn't meet the latter) run a tight ship. They know exactly what's in their inventory, the condition, and history of it.  Out of half dozen used tire shops in Sacramento that I called or emailed, this is the only one that promptly responded.

What's so hard about that? Half the reason I decided to give South West Tire my business was because of their fast, no-upsell, no-BS, no-pressure communication. Easy to get to (off 99), easy parking.

Context: I needed four matching tires for an AWD Subaru Forester with less than a year left on the lease. My current set had one that was almost bald, with the others less than 3/32". I didn't want to spring for new tires ($600+) because I'd never enjoy the full life of them. After giving me quick options based on the specs I needed, Chris and I settled on $180 for 4 matching tires (including balancing, install), 7/32" tread, that were coincidentally the OE tires (Yoko Geolandar G91s) of my lease. I was in-and-out in about 20 minutes on a quiet Sunday afternoon. I don't always buy used tires. But when I do, I'll go to South West Tire. Thanks, Chris!</Review>

<GmapID>0x80dccad4fcb0931b:0x6f289fdd766e2bb7</GmapID><user>113114927683275331828< /user>< text>
This was my first time visiting this nail salon and overall had a good experience!

Sanitation
Firstly they are doing a really nice job handling COVID. I see them sanitizing tools, chairs, and themselves after all clients. Gloves are worn by most of the staff and the chairs have built in plastic coverings that come down in front of you. Overall the location was clean and comfortable

Friendly
Both of my nail techs were friendly (Jennifer & Chau). Did a nice job of recognizing that I am not a particularly chatty patron which is a huge win in my book. They were very accommodating in ensuring i was comfortable.

Quality of Services
I personally prefer techs who are highly detail oriented and take their time. Chau did a wonderful job in responding to my needs for my pedicure. My nails are consistent and short. The gel nail polish is not thick at all (which i love), and the edges are clean and straight. Jenifer, who did my manicure was lovely, however, has some opportunity. My gel manicure was nice and thin, but the edging was not as clean as I prefer and there is some bubbling. I am certain a superior quality can be achieved with just a little more attention to detail :) In the future I would probably prefer Chau to do both.

Overall I had a good experience and would visit again!< /text>
